   var memberidtype = 'none';
var memberid = 0;
		
		function newHttpReq()
		{
			var newRequest = null;
			
			try
			{
				newRequest = new XMLHttpRequest();
			}
			catch(trymicrosoft)
			{
				try
				{
					newRequest = new ActiveXObject("Msxml2.XMLHTTP");
				}
				catch(othermicrosoft)
				{
					try
					{
						newRequest = new ActiveXObject("Microsoft.XMLHTTP");
					}
					catch(failed)
					{
						newRequest = null;
					}			
				}
			}
			
			return newRequest;

		}


		var httpobject = [];
		var requestcount = 0;	
		
		function showlogindiv(showerrors)
		{
			var backgroundobject = document.getElementById('dimdiv');
			//backgroundobject.style.display = 'block';
			backgroundobject.style.width = '100%';
			backgroundobject.style.height = '100%';
			backgroundobject.style.visibility = 'visible';		
					
			var widthclient = parseInt(document.documentElement.clientWidth);
			var heightclient = parseInt(document.documentElement.clientHeight);
			
			var widthtarget = 400;
			var heighttarget = 400;
			
			var offsetleft = 0;
			var offsettop = 0;

			if(document.documentElement.scrollTop &amp;&amp; !document.body.scrollTop)
			{
				offsetleft = document.documentElement.scrollLeft;
				offsettop = document.documentElement.scrollTop;
			}
			else
			{
				offsetleft = document.body.scrollLeft;
				offsettop = document.body.scrollTop;
			}		
			
			var logindiv = document.getElementById('logindiv');
			logindiv.style.width = widthtarget + 'px';
			logindiv.style.height = heighttarget + 'px';
			logindiv.style.visibility = 'visible';
			logindiv.innerHTML = "&lt;img src='../Searching.gif' style='float: left;'&gt;";
			
			logindiv.style.left = (offsetleft + parseInt((widthclient - widthtarget) / 2)) + 'px';
			logindiv.style.top = (offsettop + parseInt((heightclient - heighttarget) / 2)) + 'px';

			var localvalue = requestcount;
			
			httpobject[localvalue] = newHttpReq();			
			httpobject[localvalue].onreadystatechange = function(){
			
				try 
				{
					if(httpobject[localvalue].readyState == 4)
					{
					}
				
					if(httpobject[localvalue].status == 200)
					{
					}
				}
				catch (e)
				{
					return;
				}
				
				if(httpobject[localvalue].readyState == 4 &amp;&amp; httpobject[localvalue].status == 200)
				{
					document.getElementById('logindiv').innerHTML = httpobject[localvalue].responseText;
				}
			
			
			};		

			var url = "../queries/queryloginfacebook.php";
			var poststring = "showerrors=" + showerrors;

			httpobject[localvalue].open('post',url,true);
			httpobject[localvalue].setRequestHeader('content-type', 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded');
			httpobject[localvalue].send(poststring);	

			requestcount += 1;		
			
			return;	
		}
		
		
		function hidelogindiv()
		{
			document.getElementById('dimdiv').style.visibility = 'hidden';
			document.getElementById('logindiv').style.visibility = 'hidden';
			document.getElementById('logindiv').innerHTML = '&nbsp;';
		}
		
		function facebooklogin()
		{

			FB.login(function(response) {
			  if (response.session) {
				if (response.perms) {
				  // user is logged in and granted some permissions.
				  // perms is a comma separated list of granted permissions

				  //alert(response.perms);
				  
				  if(response.perms.indexOf('email') != -1)
				  {
					//alert('permission granted');
					
					document.getElementById('logindiv').innerHTML = "&lt;img src='../Searching.gif' style='float: left;'&gt;";
					
				  
					FB.getLoginStatus(function(response) {
					
						//alert(response.status);
						//alert(response.session.uid);
						//alert(response.session.access_token);
					
						var facebookuserid = response.session.uid;
						var facebookaccesstoken = response.session.access_token;
						var email = '';
					
						FB.api('/me', {access_token: facebookaccesstoken}, function(response) {
						
						var poststring = 'facebookuserid=' + facebookuserid + '&amp;facebookaccesstoken=' + facebookaccesstoken + '&amp;email=' + response.email + '&amp;firstname=' + response.first_name + '&amp;lastname=' + response.last_name + '&amp;targetfunction=' + targetfunction;
						//alert(poststring);

						var localvalue = requestcount;
						
						httpobject[localvalue] = newHttpReq();			
						httpobject[localvalue].onreadystatechange = function(){
						
							try 
							{
								if(httpobject[localvalue].readyState == 4)
								{
								}
							
								if(httpobject[localvalue].status == 200)
								{
								}
							}
							catch (e)
							{
								return;
							}
							
							if(httpobject[localvalue].readyState == 4 &amp;&amp; httpobject[localvalue].status == 200)
							{
								var response = httpobject[localvalue].responseText.split("&lt;EXTRAINSTRUCTIONS&gt;");
							
								document.getElementById('logindiv').innerHTML = response[0];
								
								if(response[1])
								{
									eval(response[1]);
								}							

							}
						
						
						};		

						var url = "../queries/queryloginfacebookcomplete.php";

						httpobject[localvalue].open('post',url,true);
						httpobject[localvalue].setRequestHeader('content-type', 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded');
						httpobject[localvalue].send(poststring);	

						requestcount += 1;	

						
						});

					});			  
				  
				  }
				  else
				  {
					alert('permission denied');
				  }
				  
				} else {
				  // user is logged in, but did not grant any permissions
				  
				   //alert('logged in: permission denied');
				  
				}
			  } else {
				// user is not logged in
				//alert('not logged in: permission denied');
			  }
			}, {scope:'publish_stream,email'});

		}


		function submitlogin()
		{

			document.getElementById('submitlogindiv').innerHTML = "&lt;img src='../Searching.gif' style='float: right;'&gt;\n";
		
			var localvalue = requestcount;
			
			httpobject[localvalue] = newHttpReq();			
			httpobject[localvalue].onreadystatechange = function(){
			
				try 
				{
					if(httpobject[localvalue].readyState == 4)
					{
					}
				
					if(httpobject[localvalue].status == 200)
					{
					}
				}
				catch (e)
				{
					return;
				}
				
				if(httpobject[localvalue].readyState == 4 &amp;&amp; httpobject[localvalue].status == 200)
				{
					var response = httpobject[localvalue].responseText.split("&lt;EXTRAINSTRUCTIONS&gt;");
				
					document.getElementById('logindiv').innerHTML = response[0];
					
					if(response[1])
					{
						eval(response[1]);
					}							

				}
			
			
			};		

			var poststring = 'username=' + document.getElementById('username').value + '&amp;password=' + document.getElementById('password').value + '&amp;sourcepage=artworkpage&amp;targetfunction=' + targetfunction;
			
			//alert(poststring);
			//return;
			
			var url = "../loginvalidationnew.php";

			httpobject[localvalue].open('post',url,true);
			httpobject[localvalue].setRequestHeader('content-type', 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded');
			httpobject[localvalue].send(poststring);	

			requestcount += 1;	
		
		}
		
		
		function favoriteimage(artworkid)
		{
			if(memberidtype == 'none')
			{
				targetfunction = "favoriteimage(" + artworkid + ")";
				showlogindiv(false);
				return;
			}

			document.getElementById('favoritediv').innerHTML = "&lt;img src='../Searching.gif' style='float: left; padding-left: 5px;'&gt;\n";
		
			var localvalue = requestcount;
			
			httpobject[localvalue] = newHttpReq();			
			httpobject[localvalue].onreadystatechange = function(){
			
				try 
				{
					if(httpobject[localvalue].readyState == 4)
					{
					}
				
					if(httpobject[localvalue].status == 200)
					{
					}
				}
				catch (e)
				{
					return;
				}
				
				if(httpobject[localvalue].readyState == 4 &amp;&amp; httpobject[localvalue].status == 200)
				{
					var response = httpobject[localvalue].responseText.split("&lt;EXTRAINSTRUCTIONS&gt;");
				
					document.getElementById('favoritediv').innerHTML = response[0];
					
					if(response[1])
					{
						eval(response[1]);
					}							

				}
			
			
			};		

			var poststring = 'artworkid=' + artworkid;
			
			//alert(poststring);
			//return;
			
			var url = '../queries/queryaddtofavoritesnew.php';

			httpobject[localvalue].open('post',url,true);
			httpobject[localvalue].setRequestHeader('content-type', 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded');
			httpobject[localvalue].send(poststring);	

			requestcount += 1;			
		}
		
		
		function showcomment1()
		{
			
			if(memberidtype == 'none')
			{
				targetfunction = "showcomment1()";
				showlogindiv(false);
				return;
			}
			
			if(document.getElementById('comment1div').getAttribute('activestatus') == 0)
			{
				document.getElementById('comment1div').style.height = '150px';
				document.getElementById('comment1div').setAttribute('activestatus',1);
				//document.getElementById('comment1div').scrollIntoView(true);
			}
			else
			{
				document.getElementById('comment1div').style.height = '0px';
				document.getElementById('comment1div').setAttribute('activestatus',0);			
			}
			
		}
		
		function submitcomment1()
		{
			var comment = document.getElementById('comment1').value;
			
			if(comment.length &lt; 3)
			{
				alert('You must enter at least three characters.');
				return;
			}
			
			document.getElementById('comment1form').submit();
		
		}
		

		function showcomment2()
		{

			if(memberidtype == 'none')
			{
				targetfunction = "showcomment2()";
				showlogindiv(false);
				return;
			}	
		
			if(document.getElementById('comment2div').getAttribute('activestatus') == 0)
			{
				document.getElementById('comment2div').style.height = '150px';
				document.getElementById('comment2div').setAttribute('activestatus',1);
				document.getElementById('comment2div').scrollIntoView(true);
			}
			else
			{
				document.getElementById('comment2div').style.height = '0px';
				document.getElementById('comment2div').setAttribute('activestatus',0);			
			}

		}

		function showreply(id)
		{

			if(document.getElementById('replydiv'))
			{
				var parentobject = document.getElementById('replydiv').parentNode;
				parentobject.removeChild(document.getElementById('replydiv'));
				
				if(id == replyid)
				{
					return;
				}
			}
			
			replyid = id;
		
			var parentobject = document.getElementById('individualcommentdiv['+id+']');
			
			var newelement = document.createElement('div');
			newelement.id = 'replydiv';
			newelement.style.styleFloat = 'left';
			newelement.style.width = '100%';
			newelement.innerHTML = "&lt;div style='float: left; width: 100%; padding-top: 20px;'&gt;&lt;form id='replyform' name='replyform' method='post' action='../validatepostcommentreply.php'&gt;&lt;input type='hidden' id='childof' name='childof' value='" + replyid + "'&gt;&lt;input type='hidden' id='artworkid' name='artworkid' value='7685095'&gt;&lt;p style='float: left; width: 100%; font: 8pt arial; font-weight: bold;'&gt;Post Reply&lt;/p&gt;&lt;div style='float: left; width: 100%; padding-top: 5px;'&gt;&lt;textarea id='reply' name='reply' style='float: left; width: 290px; padding: 5px; font: 10pt arial;'&gt;&lt;/textarea&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div style='float: left; width: 100%; padding-top: 10px;'&gt;&lt;a class='button' href='javascript: submitreply();'&gt;&lt;span&gt;Reply&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/form&gt;&lt;/div&gt;";
			
			parentobject.appendChild(newelement);		
			
		}

		function submitreply()
		{
			var comment = document.getElementById('reply').value;
			
			if(comment.length &lt; 3)
			{
				alert('You must enter at least three characters.');
				return;
			}
			
			document.getElementById('replyform').submit();
		
		}	

		function confirmdeleteimage(id)
		{
			result = confirm ('Are you sure you want to delete this image?');
			
			if (result == true)
			{
				document.getElementById('deletebuttondiv').innerHTML = "&lt;img src='../Searching.gif' style='float: left; padding-left: 5px; padding-top: 2px;'&gt;";
			
				locationstring = "../featured/guido-montanes-castillo.html?delete=true";
				document.location = locationstring;	
			}
			
		}

   <div style="float: left; width: 100%; padding-bottom: 35px; text-align: center;">
    <h1 style="float: left; width: 100%; padding-bottom: 10px; border-bottom: 2px solid #999999; font-size: 24pt; font-family: oswald, arial; font-weight: normal;">
     Recently Sold - April 23rd, 2014
    </h1>
    <p style="float: left; width: 100%; padding-top: 10px; font: 16pt arial; font-weight: normal; color: #444444;">
     Guido Montanes Castillo sold a 28.25" x 30.00" print of
     <a href="featured/the-cure-for-anything-is-salt-water-sweat-tears-or-the-sea-guido-montanes-castillo.html" style="font: inherit; font-weight: bold; color: #222222; text-decoration: none;">
      The cure for anything is salt water sweat tears or the sea
     </a>
     to a buyer from Menlo Park, CA.
    </p>
   </div>
   <div style="float: left; width: 550px;">
    <div style="float: left; width: 550px;">
     <a href="featured/the-cure-for-anything-is-salt-water-sweat-tears-or-the-sea-guido-montanes-castillo.html">
      <img src="orderimages-5/large-line-item-572777.jpg" style="float: left; max-width: 100%; padding: none; border: none; box-shadow: none;"/>
     </a>
     <div style="float: left; width: 100%; padding-top: 10px;">
      <p style="float: left; width: 100%; font-size: 14pt; font-family: oswald, arial; color: #444444;">
       <a href="featured/the-cure-for-anything-is-salt-water-sweat-tears-or-the-sea-guido-montanes-castillo.html" style="font-size: inherit; font-family: inherit; color: inherit; text-decoration: inherit;">
        The cure for anything is salt water sweat tears or the sea
       </a>
      </p>
      <p style="float: left; width: 100%; font: 9pt arial; color: #444444;">
       <a href="profiles/guido-montanes-castillo.html" style="font: inherit; color: inherit; text-decoration: inherit;">
        Guido Montanes Castillo
       </a>
      </p>
     </div>
    </div>
   </div>
   <div style="float: right; width: 320px;">
    <a href="profiles/guido-montanes-castillo.html" style="font: 14pt arial; text-decoration: underline;">
     <img src="images/artistlogos/guido-montanes-castillo-1398182379-square.jpg" style="float: left; width: 100px; height: 100px; border: 1px solid #DDDDDD; border-radius: 2px; box-shadow: 0px 8px 8px -5px #EEEEEE;"/>
    </a>
    <div style="float: left; width: 180px; overflow: hidden; padding-left: 25px;">
     <p style="float: left; width: 100%; font-size: 16pt; font-family: oswald, arial; color: #444444;">
      <a href="profiles/guido-montanes-castillo.html" style="font-size: inherit; font-family: inherit; color: inherit; text-decoration: inherit;">
       Guido Montanes Castillo
      </a>
     </p>
     <p style="float: left; width: 100%; padding-top: 10px; font: 9pt arial; color: #444444;">
      IMPORTANT! Watermark is only here you will not see it in your print.
Professional photographer.
Specialties: nature photography, aerial, architectural, historical and artistic heritage.
Publication...
     </p>
    </div>
    <div style="float: left; width: 100%; padding-top: 35px;">
     <p style="float: left; width: 100%; padding-bottom: 5px; border-bottom: 2px solid #999999; font-size: 14pt; font-family: oswald, arial; color: #444444; text-shadow: none;">
      Help Guido Spread the Word!
